        ( function () {
            "use strict";

            tdLocalCache = {
                data: {},
                remove: function (resource_id) {
                    delete tdLocalCache.data[resource_id];
                },
                exist: function (resource_id) {
                    return tdLocalCache.data.hasOwnProperty(resource_id) && tdLocalCache.data[resource_id] !== null;
                },
                get: function (resource_id) {
                    return tdLocalCache.data[resource_id];
                },
                set: function (resource_id, cachedData) {
                    tdLocalCache.remove(resource_id);
                    tdLocalCache.data[resource_id] = cachedData;
                }

       <script type="text/javascript">
        function googleTranslateElementInit2() {new google.translate.TranslateElement({pageLanguage: 'en',autoDisplay: false}, 'google_translate_element2');}
       </script>
       <script src="//translate.google.com/translate_a/element.js?cb=googleTranslateElementInit2" type="text/javascript">
       </script>
       <script type="text/javascript">
        function GTranslateFireEvent(element,event){try{if(document.createEventObject){var evt=document.createEventObject();element.fireEvent('on'+event,evt)}else{var evt=document.createEvent('HTMLEvents');evt.initEvent(event,true,true);element.dispatchEvent(evt)}}catch(e){}}function doGTranslate(lang_pair){if(lang_pair.value)lang_pair=lang_pair.value;if(lang_pair=='')return;var lang=lang_pair.split('|')[1];var teCombo;var sel=document.getElementsByTagName('select');for(var i=0;i<sel.length;i++)if(sel[i].className=='goog-te-combo')teCombo=sel[i];if(document.getElementById('google_translate_element2')==null||document.getElementById('google_translate_element2').innerHTML.length==0||teCombo.length==0||teCombo.innerHTML.length==0){setTimeout(function(){doGTranslate(lang_pair)},500)}else{teCombo.value=lang;GTranslateFireEvent(teCombo,'change');GTranslateFireEvent(teCombo,'change')}}
function GTranslateGetCurrentLang() {var keyValue = document.cookie.match('(^|;) ?googtrans=([^;]*)(;|$)');return keyValue ? keyValue[2].split('/')[2] : null;}
if(GTranslateGetCurrentLang() != null)jQuery(document).ready(function() {jQuery('div.switcher div.selected a').html(jQuery('div.switcher div.option').find('span.gflag img[alt="'+GTranslateGetCurrentLang()+'"]').parent().parent().html());});
       </script>

              <div class="item-details">
               <h3 class="entry-title td-module-title">
                <a href="https://www.madinamerica.com/2021/03/mental-health-survival-kit-chapter-2-part-3/" rel="bookmark" title="Mental Health Survival Kit, Chapter 2: Is Psychiatry Evidence Based? (Part 3)">
                 Mental Health Survival Kit, Chapter 2: Is Psychiatry Evidence Based? (Part 3)
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="td-module-meta-info">
                <span class="td-post-author-name">
                 <a class="author url fn" href="https://www.madinamerica.com/author/pgotzsche/" rel="author" title="Posts by Peter C. Gøtzsche, MD">
                  Peter C. Gøtzsche, MD
                 </a>
                 <span>
                  -
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span class="td-post-date">
                 <time class="entry-date updated td-module-date" datetime="2021-03-22T13:00:25+00:00">
                  March 22, 2021
                 </time>
                </span>
                <div class="td-module-comments">
                 <a href="https://www.madinamerica.com/2021/03/mental-health-survival-kit-chapter-2-part-3/#respond">
                  0
                 </a>
                </div>
               </div>
               <div class="td-excerpt">
                Virtually every single placebo-controlled drug trial in psychiatry is flawed, systematic reviews of trials are also flawed, and guidelines are flawed. Even the drug approval process is flawed.
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>

                 <img alt="" class="entry-thumb" height="150" src="https://www.madinamerica.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/IMG_0130-218x150.jpg" title="Online Exhibition: Art-Making During the Pandemic" width="218"/>
                </a>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="item-details">
               <h3 class="entry-title td-module-title">
                <a href="https://www.madinamerica.com/2021/03/art-making-during-the-pandemic/" rel="bookmark" title="Online Exhibition: Art-Making During the Pandemic">
                 Online Exhibition: Art-Making During the Pandemic
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="td-module-meta-info">
                <span class="td-post-author-name">
                 <a class="author url fn" href="https://www.madinamerica.com/author/kjervert/" rel="author" title="Posts by Karin Jervert">
                  Karin Jervert
                 </a>
                 <span>
                  -
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span class="td-post-date">
                 <time class="entry-date updated td-module-date" datetime="2021-03-21T06:01:23+00:00">
                  March 21, 2021
                 </time>
                </span>
                <div class="td-module-comments">
                 <a href="https://www.madinamerica.com/2021/03/art-making-during-the-pandemic/#respond">
                  0
                 </a>
                </div>
               </div>
               <div class="td-excerpt">
                The online exhibition "Creativity and COVID: Art-Making During the Pandemic" features nearly 100 artists with lived experience with mental distress who shared with us their art-making process and how it helped them survive the global pandemic.
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="td-block-span4">
             <div class="td_module_mx7 td_module_wrap td-animation-stack">
              <div class="td-module-image">
               <div class="td-module-thumb">
                <a href="https://www.madinamerica.com/2021/03/thief-hospital/" rel="bookmark" title="A Thief in the Hospital">
                 <img alt="" class="entry-thumb" height="150" src="https://www.madinamerica.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Depositphotos_181183934_s-2019-218x150.jpg" title="A Thief in the Hospital" width="218"/>
                </a>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="item-details">
               <h3 class="entry-title td-module-title">
                <a href="https://www.madinamerica.com/2021/03/thief-hospital/" rel="bookmark" title="A Thief in the Hospital">
                 A Thief in the Hospital
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="td-module-meta-info">
                <span class="td-post-author-name">
                 <a class="author url fn" href="https://www.madinamerica.com/author/enetchitailova/" rel="author" title="Posts by Ekaterina Netchitailova, PhD">
                  Ekaterina Netchitailova, PhD
                 </a>
                 <span>
                  -
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span class="td-post-date">
                 <time class="entry-date updated td-module-date" datetime="2021-03-20T13:00:04+00:00">
                  March 20, 2021
                 </time>
                </span>
                <div class="td-module-comments">
                 <a href="https://www.madinamerica.com/2021/03/thief-hospital/#comments">
                  6
                 </a>
                </div>
               </div>
               <div class="td-excerpt">
                I knew by then that there was a thief, but I tried not to rush to conclusions. I couldn’t even think of the possibility that it could be one of the staff. They go into the field in order to help people.
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>

                </a>

               <div class="td-module-meta-info">

                <a href="https://www.madinamerica.com/2021/03/psychiatry-real-illnesses/" rel="bookmark" title="How Psychiatry Turned General Difficulties in Adaptation into “Real Illnesses Just Like Diabetes”">
                 How Psychiatry Turned General Difficulties in Adaptation into “Real Illnesses Just Like Diabetes”
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="td-module-meta-info">
                <span class="td-post-author-name">
                 <a class="author url fn" href="https://www.madinamerica.com/author/philiphickey/" rel="author" title="Posts by Philip Hickey, PhD">
                  Philip Hickey, PhD
                 </a>
                 <span>
                  -
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span class="td-post-date">
                 <time class="entry-date updated td-module-date" datetime="2021-03-16T13:00:17+00:00">
                  March 16, 2021
                 </time>
                </span>
                <div class="td-module-comments">
                 <a href="https://www.madinamerica.com/2021/03/psychiatry-real-illnesses/#comments">
                  35
                 </a>
                </div>
               </div>
               <div class="td-excerpt">
                Though many psychiatrists have abandoned the "chemical imbalance" concept, they now promote the use of a pre-scientific notion that the only criteria for defining disease is the presence of distress or impairment.
               </div>

               <a class="envira-gallery-216127 envira-gallery-link envira-gallery-video" data-caption="More than 220 people from 13 different countries answered Carina Håkansson's invitation to Gothenburg to hear about and discuss research findings, new knowledge, and future directions regarding the risks of psychopharmaceuticals, and alternatives to the biological model of psychiatry. The result of the weekend was the new International Institute for Psychiatric Drug Withdrawal (IIPDW). Members of the Institute faculty are Olga Runciman, Sami Timimi, Birgitta Alakare, Robert Whitaker, Will Hall, Carina Håkansson, Jaakko Seikkula, Volkmar Aderhold, John Read, Peter Gøtzsche and Magnus Hald. 		(function(){
			var html_jquery_obj = jQuery('html');

			if (html_jquery_obj.length && (html_jquery_obj.is('.ie8') || html_jquery_obj.is('.ie9'))) {

				var path = 'https://www.madinamerica.com/wp-content/themes/mia-newspaper/style.css';

				jQuery.get(path, function(data) {

					var str_split_separator = '#td_css_split_separator';
					var arr_splits = data.split(str_split_separator);
					var arr_length = arr_splits.length;

					if (arr_length > 1) {

						var dir_path = 'https://www.madinamerica.com/wp-content/themes/Newspaper';
						var splited_css = '';

						for (var i = 0; i < arr_length; i++) {
							if (i > 0) {
								arr_splits[i] = str_split_separator + ' ' + arr_splits[i];
							}
							//jQuery('head').append('<style>' + arr_splits[i] + '</style>');

							var formated_str = arr_splits[i].replace(/\surl\(\'(?!data\:)/gi, function regex_function(str) {
								return ' url(\'' + dir_path + '/' + str.replace(/url\(\'/gi, '').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/gm,'');
							});

							splited_css += "<style>" + formated_str + "</style>";
						}

						var td_theme_css = jQuery('link#td-theme-css');

						if (td_theme_css.length) {
							td_theme_css.after(splited_css);
						}
					}
				});
			}
		})();
